Since the game is uncopylocked, we can use the roblox api to download old versions

<code class="chatlog__markdown-pre chatlog__markdown-pre--inline">https://assetdelivery.roblox.com/v1/asset/?id=ID&amp;version=VERSION</code>

There are three version, with v1 being a baseplate and v3 being the current version.

<code class="chatlog__markdown-pre chatlog__markdown-pre--inline">https://assetdelivery.roblox.com/v1/asset/?id=ID&amp;version=VERSION</code>
